				var normalize = function( term ) {
					var ret = "";
					for ( var i = 0; i < term.length; i++ ) {
						ret += accentMap[ term.charAt(i) ] || term.charAt(i);
					}
					return ret;
				}
	
				// Create autocomplete instances.
				$(function() {
					$('.buscadorEnfermedades #enfermedades').autocomplete({
						source: function( request, response ) {
							var matcher = new RegExp( $.ui.autocomplete.escapeRegex( request.term ), "i" );
							response($.grep(listadoEnfermedades, function(val) {
								return matcher.test(val.value) || matcher.test(normalize(val.value));
								}) 
							);
						},
						select: function( event, ui ) {window.location.href=ui.item.url;},
					});
				});
			});
			
			//-->
		</script>
